GoToNamedRegionAction extends EditorAction {\n\n\tconstructor() {\n\t\tsuper({\n\t\t\tid: 'editor.action.goToNamedRegion',\n\t\t\tlabel: nls.localize2('goToNamedRegion.label', \"Go to Named Region\"),\n\t\t\tprecondition: CONTEXT_FOLDING_ENABLED,\n\t\t\tkbOpts: {\n\t\t\t\tkbExpr: EditorContextKeys.editorTextFocus,\n\t\t\t\tprimary: KeyMod.CtrlCmd | KeyMod.Shift | KeyCode.KeyR,\n\t\t\t\tweight: KeybindingWeight.EditorContrib\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t});\n\t}\n\n\tpublic override runEditorCommand(accessor: ServicesAccessor, editor: ICodeEditor): void | Promise<void> {\n\t\tconst quickInputService = accessor.get(IQuickInputService);\n\t\tconst foldingController = FoldingController.get(editor);\n\n\t\tif (!foldingController) {\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tconst model = editor.getModel();\n\t\tif (!model) {\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Detect named regions in the current model\n\t\tconst namedRegionProvider = new NamedRegionProvider(model, { limit: 5000, update: () => { } });\n\t\tconst regions = namedRegionProvider.detectNamedRegions();\n\n\t\tif (regions.length === 0) {\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Create quick pick items\n\t\tconst items: IQuickPickItem[] = regions.map(region => ({\n\t\t\tlabel: region.name,\n\t\t\tdescription: `Line ${region.startLineNumber} - ${region.endLineNumber}`,\n\t\t\tdetail: undefined\n\t\t}));\n\n\t\t// Show quick pick and handle selection\n\t\tconst promise = quickInputService.pick(items, {\n\t\t\tplaceHolder: 'Go to Named Region',\n\t\t\tmatchOnDescription: true\n\t\t});\n\n\t\treturn promise.then(selectedItem => {\n\t\t\tif (selectedItem) {\n\t\t\t\tconst selectedIndex = items.indexOf(selectedItem);\n\t\t\t\tif (selectedIndex >= 0 && selectedIndex < regions.length) {\n\t\t\t\t\tconst region = regions[selectedIndex];\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// Navigate to the region\n\t\t\t\t\tconst position = new (require('../../../common/core/position.js').Position)(region.startLineNumber, 1);\n\t\t\t\t\teditor.setPosition(position);\n\t\t\t\t\teditor.revealLineInCenter(region.startLineNumber, ScrollType.Smooth);\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// Unfold the region if it's folded\n\t\t\t\t\treturn foldingController.getFoldingModel().then(foldingModel => {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif (foldingModel) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tconst regions_obj = foldingModel.regions;\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tconst regionIndex = regions_obj.findRange(region.startLineNumber);\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif (regionIndex >= 0 && regions_obj.isCollapsed(regionIndex)) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tregions_obj.setCollapsed(regionIndex, false);\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tfoldingController.triggerFoldingModelChanged();\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t});\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t});\n\t}\n\n\tprivate detectNamedRegions(model: ITextModel): Array<{ name: string; startLineNumber: number; endLineNumber: number }> {\n\t\tconst regions: Array<{ name: string; startLineNumber: number; endLineNumber: number }> = [];\n\t\tconst stack: { name: string; startLineNumber: number }[] = [];\n\n\t\tconst regionStartPattern = /^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#region\\s*(.*?)\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/;\n\t\tconst regionEndPattern = /^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#endregion\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/;\n\n\t\tfor (let lineNumber = 1; lineNumber <= model.getLineCount(); lineNumber++) {\n\t\t\tconst lineContent = model.getLineContent(lineNumber);\n\n\t\t\tconst startMatch = lineContent.match(regionStartPattern);\n\t\t\tif (startMatch) {\n\t\t\t\tconst regionName = startMatch[2] || 'Region';\n\t\t\t\tstack.push({ name: regionName.trim(), startLineNumber: lineNumber });\n\t\t\t\tcontinue;\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tconst endMatch = lineContent.match(regionEndPattern);\n\t\t\tif (endMatch && stack.length > 0) {\n\t\t\t\tconst startRegion = stack.pop()!;\n\t\t\t\tregions.push({\n\t\t\t\t\tname: startRegion.name,\n\t\t\t\t\tstartLineNumber: GoToNamedRegionAction extends EditorAction {\n\n\tconstructor() {\n\t\tsuper({\n\t\t\tid: 'editor.action.goToNamedRegion',\n\t\t\tlabel: nls.localize2('goToNamedRegion.label', \"Go to Named {\n\t\tconst quickInputService = accessor.get(IQuickInputService);\n\t\tconst foldingController = FoldingController.get(editor);\n\n\t\tif (!foldingController) {\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tconst (require('../../../common/core/position.js').Position)(region.startLineNumber, 1);\n\t\t\t\t\teditor.setPosition(position);\n\t\t\t\t\teditor.revealLineInCenter(region.startLineNumber, ScrollType.Smooth);\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// Unfold the region if it's folded\n\t\t\t\t\treturn foldingController.getFoldingModel().then(foldingModel => {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif (foldingModel) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tconst false);\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tfoldingController.triggerFoldingModelChanged();\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t});\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t});\n\t}\n\n\tprivate detectNamedRegions(model: ITextModel): Array<{ name: string; startLineNumber: number; endLineNumber: number }> {\n\t\tconst regions: Array<{ name: string; startLineNumber: number; endLineNumber: number }> = [];\n\t\tconst stack: { name: string; startLineNumber: number }[] = [];\n\n\t\tconst regionStartPattern = /^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#region\\s*(.*?)\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/;\n\t\tconst regionEndPattern = /^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#endregion\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/;\n\n\t\tfor (let lineNumber = 1; lineNumber <= model.getLineCount(); lineNumber++) {\n\t\t\tconst lineContent = 'Region';\n\t\t\t\tstack.push({ name: regionName.trim(), startLineNumber: lineNumber });\n\t\t\t\tcontinue;\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tconst endMatch = lineContent.match(regionEndPattern);\n\t\t\tif (endMatch && stack.length > 0) {\n\t\t\t\tconst startRegion = stack.pop()!;\n\t\t\t\tregions.push({\n\t\t\t\t\tname: startRegion.name,\n\t\t\t\t\tstartLineNumber: startRegion.startLineNumber,\n\t\t\t\t\tendLineNumber: lineNumber\n\t\t\t\t});\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn regions;\n\t}\n}\n\n\nregisterEditorContribution(FoldingController.ID, FoldingController, GoToNamedRegionAction extends EditorAction {\n\n\tconstructor() {\n\t\tsuper({\n\t\t\tid: 'editor.action.goToNamedRegion',\n\t\t\tlabel: nls.localize2('goToNamedRegion.label', \"Go to Named Region\"),\n\t\t\tprecondition: CONTEXT_FOLDING_ENABLED,\n\t\t\tkbOpts: {\n\t\t\t\tkbExpr: EditorContextKeys.editorTextFocus,\n\t\t\t\tprimary: KeyMod.CtrlCmd | KeyMod.Shift | KeyCode.KeyR,\n\t\t\t\tweight: KeybindingWeight.EditorContrib\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t});\n\t}\n\n\tpublic override runEditorCommand(accessor: ServicesAccessor, editor: ICodeEditor): void | Promise<void> {\n\t\tconst quickInputService = accessor.get(IQuickInputService);\n\t\tconst foldingController = FoldingController.get(editor);\n\n\t\tif (!foldingController) {\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tconst model = editor.getModel();\n\t\tif (!model) {\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Detect named regions in the current model\n\t\tconst namedRegionProvider = new NamedRegionProvider(model, { limit: 5000, update: () => { } });\n\t\tconst regions = namedRegionProvider.detectNamedRegions();\n\n\t\tif (regions.length === 0) {\n\t\t\treturn;\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Create quick pick items\n\t\tconst items: IQuickPickItem[] = regions.map(region => ({\n\t\t\tlabel: region.name,\n\t\t\tdescription: `Line ${region.startLineNumber} - ${region.endLineNumber}`,\n\t\t\tdetail: undefined\n\t\t}));\n\n\t\t// Show quick pick and handle selection\n\t\tconst promise = quickInputService.pick(items, {\n\t\t\tplaceHolder: 'Go to Named Region',\n\t\t\tmatchOnDescription: true\n\t\t});\n\n\t\treturn promise.then(selectedItem => {\n\t\t\tif (selectedItem) {\n\t\t\t\tconst selectedIndex = items.indexOf(selectedItem);\n\t\t\t\tif (selectedIndex >= 0 && selectedIndex < regions.length) {\n\t\t\t\t\tconst region = regions[selectedIndex];\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// Navigate to the region\n\t\t\t\t\tconst position = new Position(region.startLineNumber, 1);\n\t\t\t\t\teditor.setPosition(position);\n\t\t\t\t\teditor.revealLineInCenter(region.startLineNumber, ScrollType.Smooth);\n\n\t\t\t\t\t// Unfold the region if it's folded\n\t\t\t\t\treturn foldingController.getFoldingModel().then(foldingModel => {\n\t\t\t\t\t\tif (foldingModel) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tconst regions_obj = foldingModel.regions;\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tconst regionIndex = regions_obj.findRange(region.startLineNumber);\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif (regionIndex >= 0 && regions_obj.isCollapsed(regionIndex)) {\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tregions_obj.setCollapsed(regionIndex, false);\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tfoldingController.triggerFoldingModelChanged();\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\t\t});\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t});\n\t}\n\n\tprivate detectNamedRegions(model: ITextModel): Array<{ name: string; startLineNumber: number; endLineNumber: number }> {\n\t\tconst regions: Array<{ name: string; startLineNumber: number; endLineNumber: number }> = [];\n\t\tconst stack: { name: string; startLineNumber: number }[] = [];\n\n\t\tconst regionStartPattern = /^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#region\\s*(.*?)\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/;\n\t\tconst regionEndPattern = /^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#endregion\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/;\n\n\t\tfor (let lineNumber = 1; lineNumber <= model.getLineCount(); lineNumber++) {\n\t\t\tconst lineContent = model.getLineContent(lineNumber);\n\n\t\t\tconst startMatch = lineContent.match(regionStartPattern);\n\t\t\tif (startMatch) {\n\t\t\t\tconst regionName = startMatch[2] || 'Region';\n\t\t\t\tstack.push({ name: regionName.trim(), startLineNumber: lineNumber });\n\t\t\t\tcontinue;\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tconst endMatch = lineContent.match(regionEndPattern);\n\t\t\tif (endMatch && stack.length > 0) {\n\t\t\t\tconst startRegion = stack.pop()!;\n\t\t\t\tregions.push({\n\t\t\t\t\tname: startRegion.name,\n\t\t\t\t\tstartLineNumber: startRegion.startLineNumber,\n\t\t\t\t\tendLineNumber: lineNumber\n\t\t\t\t});\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn regions;\n\t}\n}\n\n\nregisterEditorContribution(FoldingController.ID, FoldingController, {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01M7vh6vK9URkyqMraX8nzpU","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01L9wXCGwEh9bdtSFPxfscaj","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/NAMED_REGIONS_IMPLEMENTATION.md","content":"# Custom Named Folding Regions Implementation\n\n## Overview\n\nThis implementation adds support for custom named folding regions in VS Code. Users can mark regions in their code with special comments (`#region Name` / `#endregion`) and navigate between them using a quick-pick menu.\n\n## Features\n\n### 1. Region Detection\nThe implementation detects regions marked with:\n- **Line comments**: `// #region MyRegionName` and `// #endregion`\n- **Block comments**: `/* #region MyRegionName */` and `/* #endregion */`\n- Supports indented markers\n- Handles nested regions correctly\n- Extracts region names from the marker text\n\n### 2. Navigation\n- **Command**: `editor.action.goToNamedRegion`\n- **Default Keybinding**: `Ctrl+Shift+R` (Windows/Linux) or `Cmd+Shift+R` (macOS)\n- Shows quick-pick menu listing all named regions\n- Each item displays the region name and line range\n- Navigates to selected region and automatically unfolds if collapsed\n\n### 3. Region Name Extraction\nWhen a region is marked like:\n```javascript\n// #region UserAuthentication\nfunction login() { ... }\n// #endregion\n```\n\nThe system extracts \"UserAuthentication\" as the region name. If no name is provided, it defaults to \"Region\".\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Files Created\n\n#### 1. `namedRegionProvider.ts`\nCore provider class implementing the `RangeProvider` interface.\n\n**Key Components:**\n- `NamedRegionProvider`: Main provider class\n- `NamedRegion`: Interface defining region structure\n  ```typescript\n  interface NamedRegion {\n    name: string;\n    startLineNumber: number;\n    endLineNumber: number;\n  }\n  ```\n\n**Methods:**\n- `detectNamedRegions()`: Scans the model and detects all named regions\n- `compute()`: Returns FoldingRegions with names stored in the types array\n- `getNamedRegions()`: Returns array of detected regions\n\n**Regex Patterns:**\n- Start: `/^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#region\\s*(.*?)\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/`\n- End: `/^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#endregion\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/`\n\n#### 2. Modified `folding.ts`\nAdded the navigation command and action:\n\n**New Class:**\n- `GoToNamedRegionAction`: Extends `EditorAction`\n  - Shows quick-pick menu with all regions\n  - Navigates to selected region\n  - Automatically unfolds collapsed regions\n\n**Changes:**\n- Added imports for `IQuickInputService`, `Position`, and `NamedRegionProvider`\n- Registered action via `registerEditorAction(GoToNamedRegionAction)`\n\n#### 3. `namedRegionProvider.test.ts`\nComprehensive test suite with 10 test cases:\n\n- ✅ Detects simple named regions with line comments\n- ✅ Detects nested named regions\n- ✅ Detects block comment regions\n- ✅ Handles default region names\n- ✅ Handles unmatched endregion gracefully\n- ✅ Detects multiple separate regions\n- ✅ Computes folding regions correctly\n- ✅ Handles empty files\n- ✅ Preserves whitespace in region names\n- ✅ Handles indented region markers\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Basic Region\n```javascript\n// #region Authentication\nfunction login(username, password) {\n  // ... authentication logic\n}\n// #endregion\n```\n\n### Nested Regions\n```javascript\n// #region UserManagement\n  // #region UserCreation\n  function createUser(userData) {\n    // ... user creation\n  }\n  // #endregion\n\n  // #region UserDeletion\n  function deleteUser(userId) {\n    // ... user deletion\n  }\n  // #endregion\n// #endregion\n```\n\n### Class Methods\n```typescript\nclass Database {\n  /* #region Connection Management */\n  connect() { }\n  disconnect() { }\n  /* #endregion */\n\n  /* #region Query Execution */\n  query() { }\n  execute() { }\n  /* #endregion */\n}\n```\n\n## How It Works\n\n### Region Detection Process\n1. Provider scans each line in the document\n2. Uses regex to identify `#region` and `#endregion` markers\n3. Maintains a stack to handle nested regions\n4. When an `#endregion` is found, pops from stack and records the region\n\n### Navigation Process\n1. User presses `Ctrl+Shift+R` (or `Cmd+Shift+R` on macOS)\n2. System detects all named regions in current document\n3. Quick-pick menu shows all regions with:\n   - Label: Region name\n   - Description: Line range (e.g., \"Line 10 - 25\")\n4. User selects a region\n5. Editor navigates to region start line and unfolds if needed\n\n## Architecture\n\n```\nEditor Input\n    ↓\nGoToNamedRegionAction (runEditorCommand)\n    ↓\nNamedRegionProvider.detectNamedRegions()\n    ↓\nParse with Regex Patterns\n    ↓\nBuild Region Stack (handles nesting)\n    ↓\nReturn NamedRegion[] array\n    ↓\nShow Quick-Pick Menu\n    ↓\nNavigate to Selected Region\n    ↓\nUnfold Region via FoldingModel\n```\n\n## Supported Languages\nThe region markers work in any text file. Language-specific comment syntax is automatically handled by the regex patterns:\n- JavaScript/TypeScript: `// #region` or `/* #region */`\n- Python: Could be extended with `# #region` (not currently implemented)\n- C/C++: Already supported with `// #region` and `/* #region */`\n\n## Performance Considerations\n- Region detection runs synchronously on demand (when action is triggered)\n- O(n) time complexity where n = number of lines\n- Efficient stack-based algorithm for nested regions\n- No background processing or continuous scanning\n\n## Extension Points\n\nFuture enhancements could include:\n1. **Region Decorations**: Display region names in the gutter or inline\n2. **Outline View Integration**: Show regions in the file outline\n3. **Breadcrumb Integration**: Display current region in breadcrumb\n4. **Region Collapsing**: Collapse all regions of a type\n5. **Language-specific Patterns**: Custom region markers per language\n6. **Region Renaming**: Rename regions with refactoring support\n\n## Testing\nRun tests with:\n```bash\nnpm run test-node -- test/unit/node/index.js\n```\n\nOr specifically for folding tests:\n```bash\nmocha src/vs/editor/contrib/folding/test/browser/namedRegionProvider.test.ts\n```\n\n## Compatibility\n- VS Code 1.96.0+\n- Works with all file types (no language-specific restrictions)\n- Compatible with existing folding providers\n- Does not interfere with syntax-based or indent-based folding\n\n## Troubleshooting\n\n### Regions Not Detected\n- Ensure region markers use correct syntax: `// #region Name`\n- Check for typos in `#region` and `#endregion`\n- Verify markers are at line start or indentation only before them\n\n### Navigation Not Working\n- Confirm folding is enabled (`editor.folding` setting)\n- Check that FoldingController is initialized\n- Ensure model is loaded in editor\n\n### Performance Issues\n- For files with very many regions (>1000), system limits to first 5000\n- Consider breaking large files into multiple Users can mark regions in their code with special comments (`#region Name` / `#endregion`) and navigate between them using a quick-pick menu.\n\n## Features\n\n### 1. Region Detection\nThe implementation detects regions marked with:\n- **Line comments**: `// #region MyRegionName` and `// #endregion`\n- **Block comments**: `/* #region MyRegionName */` and `/* #endregion */`\n- Supports indented markers\n- Handles nested regions correctly\n- Extracts region names from the marker text\n\n### 2. Navigation\n- **Command**: `editor.action.goToNamedRegion`\n- **Default Keybinding**: `Ctrl+Shift+R` (Windows/Linux) or `Cmd+Shift+R` (macOS)\n- Shows quick-pick menu listing all named regions\n- Each item displays the region name and line range\n- Navigates to selected region and automatically unfolds if collapsed\n\n### 3. Region Name Extraction\nWhen a region is marked like:\n```javascript\n// #region UserAuthentication\nfunction login() { ... }\n// #endregion\n```\n\nThe system extracts \"UserAuthentication\" as the region name. If no name is provided, it defaults to \"Region\".\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### Files Created\n\n#### 1. `namedRegionProvider.ts`\nCore provider class implementing the `RangeProvider` interface.\n\n**Key Components:**\n- `NamedRegionProvider`: Main provider class\n- `NamedRegion`: Interface defining region structure\n  ```typescript\n  interface NamedRegion {\n    name: string;\n    startLineNumber: number;\n    endLineNumber: number;\n  }\n  ```\n\n**Methods:**\n- `detectNamedRegions()`: Scans the model and detects all named regions\n- `compute()`: Returns FoldingRegions with names stored in the types array\n- `getNamedRegions()`: Returns array of detected regions\n\n**Regex Patterns:**\n- Start: `/^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#region\\s*(.*?)\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/`\n- End: `/^\\s*(\\/\\/|\\/\\*)\\s*#endregion\\s*(\\/\\*)?\\s*$/`\n\n#### 2. Modified `folding.ts`\nAdded the navigation command and action:\n\n**New Class:**\n- `GoToNamedRegionAction`: Extends `EditorAction`\n  - Shows quick-pick menu with all regions\n  - Navigates to selected region\n  - Automatically unfolds collapsed regions\n\n**Changes:**\n- Added imports for `IQuickInputService`, `Position`, and `NamedRegionProvider`\n- Registered action via `registerEditorAction(GoToNamedRegionAction)`\n\n#### 3. `namedRegionProvider.test.ts`\nComprehensive test suite with 10 test cases:\n\n- ✅ Detects simple named regions with line comments\n- ✅ Detects nested named regions\n- ✅ Detects block comment regions\n- ✅ Handles default region names\n- ✅ Handles unmatched endregion gracefully\n- ✅ Detects multiple separate regions\n- ✅ Computes folding regions correctly\n- ✅ Handles empty files\n- ✅ Preserves whitespace in region names\n- ✅ Handles indented region markers\n\n## Usage Examples\n\n### Basic Region\n```javascript\n// #region Authentication\nfunction login(username, password) {\n  // ... authentication logic\n}\n// #endregion\n```\n\n### Nested Regions\n```javascript\n// #region UserManagement\n  // #region UserCreation\n  function createUser(userData) {\n    // ... user creation\n  }\n  // #endregion\n\n  // #region UserDeletion\n  function deleteUser(userId) {\n    // ... user deletion\n  }\n  // #endregion\n// #endregion\n```\n\n### Class Methods\n```typescript\nclass Database {\n  /* #region Connection Management */\n  connect() { }\n  disconnect() { }\n  /* #endregion */\n\n  /* #region Query Execution */\n  query() { }\n  execute() { }\n  /* #endregion */\n}\n```\n\n## How It Works\n\n### Region Detection Process\n1. Provider scans each line in the document\n2. Uses regex to identify `#region` and `#endregion` markers\n3. Maintains a stack to handle nested regions\n4. When an `#endregion` is found, pops from stack and records the region\n\n### Navigation Process\n1. User presses `Ctrl+Shift+R` (or `Cmd+Shift+R` on macOS)\n2. System detects all named regions in current document\n3. Quick-pick menu shows all regions with:\n   - Label: Region name\n   - Description: Line range (e.g., \"Line 10 - 25\")\n4. User selects a region\n5. Language-specific comment syntax is automatically handled by the regex patterns:\n- JavaScript/TypeScript: `// #region` or `/* #region */`\n- Python: Could be extended with `# #region` (not currently implemented)\n- C/C++: Already supported with `// #region` and `/* #region */`\n\n## Performance Considerations\n- Region detection runs synchronously on demand (when action is triggered)\n- O(n) time complexity where n = number of lines\n- Efficient stack-based algorithm for nested regions\n- No background processing or continuous scanning\n\n## Extension Points\n\nFuture enhancements could include:\n1. **Region Decorations**: Display region names in the gutter or inline\n2. **Outline View Integration**: Show regions in the file outline\n3. **Breadcrumb Integration**: Display current
